A 500-meter walk is to the mountain gate. If you don't want to walk, there is a bus at the door. The hotel service is also very good, beyond expectations. Whether it is picking up at the station or checking in, it is very comfortable. What's especially amazing is that late-night check-in also provides midnight snacks. No one can refuse a bowl of noodles late at night, and it is still very delicious. As a senior foodie, I can give this bowl of noodles a full score! The hotel room is also very comfortable, and it also provides many activities. Hanfu copying scriptures is very interesting. The breakfast is rich and of good quality, and the coffee machine tastes OK. There is a terrace on the roof of the hotel where you can watch the sunset. When I left the hotel to climb the mountain in the morning, the hotel also provided extra water and disposable towels, which was very considerate.

msg:The hotel is located next to the main road of Nanyue, and there is a parking lot inside. The hotel is clean and tidy. The parent-child room is warmly decorated, with a 1.5-meter big bed and a 1.2-meter small bed, which solves the accommodation problem of a family of three. The bed is soft and comfortable, and it also comes with peace blessings and fruits. The toilet and bathroom are divided into dry and wet areas, the breakfast is also relatively rich, and the air conditioning in the room is very good. The most impressive thing is its service, which is very good. From the front desk reception, room service to parking security, the service attitude is very enthusiastic, which makes people feel like spring breeze. There is no place to dry clothes in the room, and the customer service immediately brought a simple clothes drying rack. If there is food that needs to be frozen, the front desk will immediately help you put it in the restaurant freezer. The service can be scored full marks. Disadvantages: The bath water is not hot enough; it would be better if there is a family room suitable for traveling with older children. The slide wastes the space of the room for families with older children, resulting in the problem of nowhere to put clothes and nowhere to sit.

Perhaps due to the Mountain Deityâ€™s Force, to dwell in this hotel three days two nights for our trip of pilgrimage proved to be auspicious and memorable. From first moment being picked up at railway station until the last minute dropped at the same station, undoubtedly the hotel has done great work, proven to be very professional in hospitality industry. The staff, no matter where they are, at reception, in dinning-hall, or by cleaning rooms - all are wearing smiling faces, performing the very cordiality and kindness. The next morning as they came to know our trip were to reach the top of the mountain simply by feet starting from the mountain-foot, surprisingly they expressed some supportive actions for our convenience. The location of the hotel is pragmatically convenient; rooms are spacious, clean and neat. The breakfast is rich and most of the foods are with chili of Hunan-style.
Thanks again to all staff for offering us the excellent service!
